 It is a part of the right posterior temporal lobe, which is one of the four major parts of the mammalian brain
 shodh main pataa chalaa he ki jin logon main khaas taur se daahine posterior temporal lob main chot lag jaati he, unhen aawaaj pahchaanane main mushkil hoti he
